    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz * u_xlat16_18.xyz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_12.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz + u_xlat16_9.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat10_5.w * _Emissive;
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_6.x * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat10_7.xyz * u_xlat16_6.xxx;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * _EmisssionColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_12.xyz = u_xlat16_12.xyz * u_xlat10_5.zzz + u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = _TimeParameters.x * _DOTEmissionQuency;
    u_xlat1.y = _TimeParameters.x * _OverlayColorQuency;
    u_xlat1.xy = sin(u_xlat1.xy);
    u_xlat16_6.x = _OverlayColor.w + (-_OverlayColorFlicker);
    u_xlat16_18.x = _OverlayColor.w + _OverlayColorFlicker;
    u_xlat16_6.x = (-u_xlat16_18.x) + u_xlat16_6.x;
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat1.y * u_xlat16_6.x + u_xlat16_18.x;
    u_xlat16_6.x = (-u_xlat16_6.x) * _Ratio_OverlayColorEffect + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_12.xyz = u_xlat16_12.xyz * u_xlat16_6.xxx;
    u_xlat16_12.xyz = _OverlayColor.xyz * vec3(_Ratio_OverlayColorEffect) + u_xlat16_12.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.x = (-u_xlat16_0.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_6.x = log2(u_xlat16_6.x);
    u_xlat16_18.x = u_xlat16_6.x * _DOTFresnelPower;
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_6.x * _flowFresnelPower;
    u_xlat16_6.x = exp2(u_xlat16_6.x);
    u_xlat16_6.y = exp2(u_xlat16_18.x);
    u_xlat16_6.xy = min(u_xlat16_6.xy, vec2(1.0, 1.0));
    u_xlat16_30 = (-_DOTEmissionMax) + _DOTEmissionMin;
    u_xlat16_30 = u_xlat1.x * u_xlat16_30 + _DOTEmissionMax;
    u_xlat16_6.xy = u_xlat16_6.xy * vec2(u_xlat16_30);
    u_xlat16_6.xzw = u_xlat16_6.xxx * _flowFresnelColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xzw = _flowColor.xyz * _flowColor.www + u_xlat16_6.xzw;
    u_xlat16_18.x = u_xlat16_6.y * _DOTEmissionScale;
    u_xlat16_18.x = u_xlat16_18.x * _Ratio_FlashColorEffect;
    u_xlat16_12.xyz = u_xlat16_18.xxx * _DOTColor.xyz + u_xlat16_12.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat1.xy = u_xlat1.xx * _flowPosition.zw + u_xlat3.xy;
    u_xlat10_1.xyz = texture2D(_AdditionalTexture, u_xlat1.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat10_1.xyz * _AddTexColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_18.x = _Ratio_ExtraTexture * _AddTexScale;
    u_xlat16_12.xyz = u_xlat16_9.xyz * u_xlat16_18.xxx + u_xlat16_12.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xzw * vec3(vec3(_Ratio_flowColor, _Ratio_flowColor, _Ratio_flowColor)) + u_xlat16_12.xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xxx * _SteadyColor.xyz + (-u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_36 = _Ratio_SteadyColorEffect * _SteadyColor.w;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_36) * u_xlat16_0.xyz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(1.12949991, 1.12949991, 1.12949991) + vec3(0.0299999993, 0.0299999993, 0.0299999993);
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(0.449999988, 0.449999988, 0.449999988);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(1.09350002, 1.09350002, 1.09350002) + vec3(0.589999974, 0.589999974, 0.589999974);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * u_xlat2.xyz + vec3(0.0799999982, 0.0799999982, 0.0799999982);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz / u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = min(u_xlat1.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz;
    SV_Target0.w = _CustomAlpha;
    return;

{

    u_xlat16_0.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;

    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = max(u_xlat1.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);

    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat3.xy = u_xlat1.xx * u_xlat4.xy;
    u_xlat3.xy = u_xlat3.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);

    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat1.xxx * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat1.x = min(max(u_xlat1.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat1.x = clamp(u_xlat1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif

    u_xlat16_5 = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_36 = u_xlat16_5.y + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_36 = max(u_xlat16_36, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_36 = min(u_xlat16_36, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_36 * u_xlat16_36;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * u_xlat16_6.x;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * u_xlat1.x + u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat16_6.x / u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat16_6.x * u_xlat16_6.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat2.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat14.x = u_xlat16_36 * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * u_xlat14.x;
    u_xlat1.x = min(u_xlat1.x, 100.0);
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_5.x + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_18.x = u_xlat16_6.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_18.x = min(max(u_xlat16_18.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_18.x = clamp(u_xlat16_18.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_6.x = (-u_xlat16_6.x) * 0.959999979 + 0.959999979;
    u_xlat16_6.x = (-u_xlat16_6.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_6.x = (-u_xlat16_36) + u_xlat16_6.x;
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_6.x + 1.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_6.x = min(max(u_xlat16_6.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_6.x = clamp(u_xlat16_6.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_7 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat14.xyz = u_xlat16_7.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat14.xyz = u_xlat16_18.xxx * u_xlat14.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_18.xyz = (-u_xlat16_7.xyz) * u_xlat16_18.xxx + u_xlat16_7.xyz;
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat1.xxx * u_xlat14.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat1.x = min(max(u_xlat1.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat1.x = clamp(u_xlat1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = (-u_xlat8.xyz) * u_xlat1.xxx + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat1.xxx * u_xlat8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat1.xxx * u_xlat16_18.xyz;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_7.www * u_xlat16_9.xyz + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_9.xyz * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;

    u_xlat16_11.xyz = min(u_xlat16_11.xyz, vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005));

    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_10.xyz * u_xlat16_11.xyz + u_xlat16_9.xyz;
    u_xlat16_45 = dot((-u_xlat13.xyz), u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat16_45 = u_xlat16_45 + u_xlat16_45;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * (-vec3(u_xlat16_45)) + (-u_xlat13.xyz);
    u_xlat16_0.x = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, u_xlat13.xyz);
    u_xlat16_0.x = abs(u_xlat16_0.x) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_0.x = min(u_xlat16_0.x, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_12.x = (-u_xlat16_36) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_12.x = u_xlat16_12.x * u_xlat16_36;
    u_xlat16_12.x = u_xlat16_12.x * 6.0;
    u_xlat16_1 = textureLod(unity_SpecCube0, u_xlat16_10.xyz, u_xlat16_12.x);
    u_xlat16_12.x = u_xlat16_1.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_12.x = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_12.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_12.x = max(u_xlat16_12.x, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_12.x = log2(u_xlat16_12.x);
    u_xlat16_12.x = u_xlat16_12.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_12.x = exp2(u_xlat16_12.x);
    u_xlat16_12.x = u_xlat16_12.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_12.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_12.xxx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_12.xyz * u_xlat2.xxx;
    u_xlat37 = (-u_xlat16_0.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_12.x = u_xlat37 * u_xlat37;
    u_xlat16_12.x = u_xlat16_12.x * u_xlat16_12.x;
    u_xlat4.xyz = (-u_xlat14.xyz) + u_xlat16_6.xxx;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat16_12.xxx * u_xlat4.xyz + u_xlat14.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz * u_xlat16_18.xyz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_12.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz + u_xlat16_9.xyz;

    u_xlat1.x = _TimeParameters.x * _DOTEmissionQuency;
    u_xlat1.y = _TimeParameters.x * _OverlayColorQuency;

    u_xlat16_6.x = _OverlayColor.w + (-_OverlayColorFlicker);
    u_xlat16_18.x = _OverlayColor.w + _OverlayColorFlicker;
    u_xlat16_6.x = (-u_xlat16_18.x) + u_xlat16_6.x;
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat1.y * u_xlat16_6.x + u_xlat16_18.x;

    u_xlat16_12.xyz = _OverlayColor.xyz * vec3(_Ratio_OverlayColorEffect) + u_xlat16_12.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.x = (-u_xlat16_0.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_6.x = log2(u_xlat16_6.x);
    u_xlat16_18.x = u_xlat16_6.x * _DOTFresnelPower;
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_6.x * _flowFresnelPower;
    u_xlat16_6.x = exp2(u_xlat16_6.x);
    u_xlat16_6.y = exp2(u_xlat16_18.x);
    u_xlat16_6.xy = min(u_xlat16_6.xy, vec2(1.0, 1.0));
    u_xlat16_30 = (-_DOTEmissionMax) + _DOTEmissionMin;
    u_xlat16_30 = u_xlat1.x * u_xlat16_30 + _DOTEmissionMax;

SubProgram "gles " {

"// hash: f6d0245f317f88be
#ifdef VERTEX
#version 100

uniform 	vec3 _WorldSpaceCameraPos;

uniform 	mediump vec4 _SHBotColor;

attribute highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
attribute highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
attribute highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
varying highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;

mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
mediump vec2 u_xlat16_2;

vec3 u_xlat4;
float u_xlat6;
float u_xlat11;
float u_xlat15;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _BumpMap_ST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _BaseColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Emissive;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _RoughNessOffset;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _SHBotColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Metallic;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec3 _AddLightDir;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Ratio_SteadyColorEffect;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _SteadyColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Ratio_FlashColorEffect;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _DOTEmissionQuency;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _DOTFresnelPower;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _DOTEmissionMax;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _DOTEmissionMin;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _OverlayColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _OverlayColorQuency;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _OverlayColorFlicker;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Ratio_OverlayColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _DOTEmissionScale;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Ratio_OverlayColorEffect;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _MouthTiling;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _MouthOffset;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _EyeTiling;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _EyeOffset;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 _AddTexST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _AddTexColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _AddTexScale;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Ratio_ExtraTexture;

	UNITY_UNIFORM float _ChangeFace;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _EmisssionColor;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
};
#endif
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
mediump vec2 u_xlat16_2;
vec3 u_xlat3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
float u_xlat6;
float u_xlat11;
float u_xlat15;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat0.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat0.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat0.y * u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat6 = u_xlat0.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat11 = u_xlat1.x * 0.125 + u_xlat6;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * 0.125 + (-u_xlat6);
    u_xlat1.y = u_xlat1.x + 0.125;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat11 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_2.xy = max(u_xlat1.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_2.xy = u_xlat16_2.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_1 = u_xlat16_2.yyyy * _SHBotColor;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat16_2.xxxx * _SHTopColor + u_xlat16_1;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyw = (-u_xlat4.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat0.w = u_xlat1.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat0;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat2.w = u_xlat1.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat2;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat0.zxy * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.yzx * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat4.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat4.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat4.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;
}

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump samplerCube unity_SpecCube0;

in highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
in highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD8;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
vec3 u_xlat1;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
vec3 u_xlat3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_5;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_6;
vec3 u_xlat7;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_7;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_8;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_9;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_10;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_11;
vec3 u_xlat12;
vec3 u_xlat13;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_17;
mediump float u_xlat16_28;
mediump float u_xlat16_33;
float u_xlat34;
mediump float u_xlat16_41;
void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_0.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_0.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = max(u_xlat1.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat12.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * u_xlat1.xxx;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * u_xlat1.xxx + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-u_xlat12.yzx) * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].zxy;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].yzx * (-u_xlat12.zxy) + (-u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat1.xxx * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = (-u_xlat12.zxy) * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat4.xyz = (-u_xlat12.yzx) * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat1.xxx * u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_0.xy = u_xlat16_0.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_0.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.xyw = u_xlat16_0.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = u_xlat16_0.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_0.xyw;
    u_xlat16_33 = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat16_33 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_33);
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_33) * u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    u_xlat4.y = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat4.x = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat4.z = dot((-u_xlat12.xyz), u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat3.xy = u_xlat1.xx * u_xlat4.xy;
    u_xlat3.xy = u_xlat3.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = texture(_MatMap, u_xlat3.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat3.xy = u_xlat3.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vs_TEXCOORD8.xy;
    u_xlat3.xy = u_xlat3.xy * _AddTexST.xy + _AddTexST.zw;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat1.xxx * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat1.x = min(max(u_xlat1.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat1.x = clamp(u_xlat1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat2.x = (-u_xlat1.x) * u_xlat1.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_5 = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_33 = u_xlat16_5.y + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_33 = max(u_xlat16_33, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_33 = min(u_xlat16_33, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_33 * u_xlat16_33;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * u_xlat16_6.x;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * u_xlat1.x + u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat16_6.x / u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat16_6.x * u_xlat16_6.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat2.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat13.x = u_xlat16_33 * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * u_xlat13.x;
    u_xlat1.x = min(u_xlat1.x, 100.0);
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_5.x + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_17.x = u_xlat16_6.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_17.x = min(max(u_xlat16_17.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_17.x = clamp(u_xlat16_17.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_6.x = (-u_xlat16_6.x) * 0.959999979 + 0.959999979;
    u_xlat16_6.x = (-u_xlat16_6.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_6.x = (-u_xlat16_33) + u_xlat16_6.x;
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_6.x + 1.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_6.x = min(max(u_xlat16_6.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_6.x = clamp(u_xlat16_6.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_7 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat13.xyz = u_xlat16_7.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat13.xyz = u_xlat16_17.xxx * u_xlat13.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_17.xyz = (-u_xlat16_7.xyz) * u_xlat16_17.xxx + u_xlat16_7.xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat1.xxx * u_xlat13.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat1.x = min(max(u_xlat1.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat1.x = clamp(u_xlat1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = (-u_xlat7.xyz) * u_xlat1.xxx + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat1.xxx * u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat1.xxx * u_xlat16_17.xyz;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_7.www * u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_5.www * u_xlat16_8.xyz + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz * vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005);
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = min(u_xlat16_10.xyz, vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005));
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * u_xlat16_10.xyz;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_9.xyz * u_xlat16_10.xyz + u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_41 = dot((-u_xlat12.xyz), u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat16_41 = u_xlat16_41 + u_xlat16_41;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * (-vec3(u_xlat16_41)) + (-u_xlat12.xyz);
    u_xlat16_0.x = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, u_xlat12.xyz);
    u_xlat16_0.x = abs(u_xlat16_0.x) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_0.x = min(u_xlat16_0.x, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_11.x = (-u_xlat16_33) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_11.x = u_xlat16_11.x * u_xlat16_33;
    u_xlat16_11.x = u_xlat16_11.x * 6.0;
    u_xlat16_1 = textureLod(unity_SpecCube0, u_xlat16_9.xyz, u_xlat16_11.x);
    u_xlat16_11.x = u_xlat16_1.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_11.x = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_11.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_11.x = max(u_xlat16_11.x, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_11.x = log2(u_xlat16_11.x);

    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat10_1.xyz * u_xlat16_11.xxx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_11.xyz * u_xlat2.xxx;
    u_xlat4.xyz = (-u_xlat13.xyz) + u_xlat16_6.xxx;
    u_xlat34 = (-u_xlat16_0.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_11.x = u_xlat34 * u_xlat34;
    u_xlat16_11.x = u_xlat16_11.x * u_xlat16_11.x;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat16_11.xxx * u_xlat4.xyz + u_xlat13.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz * u_xlat16_17.xyz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz + u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat10_5.zzz * u_xlat16_11.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = _TimeParameters.x * _DOTEmissionQuency;
    u_xlat1.y = _TimeParameters.x * _OverlayColorQuency;
    u_xlat1.xy = sin(u_xlat1.xy);
    u_xlat16_6.x = _OverlayColor.w + (-_OverlayColorFlicker);
    u_xlat16_17.x = _OverlayColor.w + _OverlayColorFlicker;
    u_xlat16_6.x = (-u_xlat16_17.x) + u_xlat16_6.x;
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat1.y * u_xlat16_6.x + u_xlat16_17.x;
    u_xlat16_6.x = (-u_xlat16_6.x) * _Ratio_OverlayColorEffect + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat16_11.xyz * u_xlat16_6.xxx;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = _OverlayColor.xyz * vec3(_Ratio_OverlayColorEffect) + u_xlat16_11.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.x = (-u_xlat16_0.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_6.x = log2(u_xlat16_6.x);
    u_xlat16_17.x = u_xlat16_6.x * _DOTFresnelPower;
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_6.x * _flowFresnelPower;
    u_xlat16_6.x = exp2(u_xlat16_6.x);
    u_xlat16_6.y = exp2(u_xlat16_17.x);
    u_xlat16_6.xy = min(u_xlat16_6.xy, vec2(1.0, 1.0));
    u_xlat16_28 = (-_DOTEmissionMax) + _DOTEmissionMin;
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat1.x * u_xlat16_28 + _DOTEmissionMax;
    u_xlat16_6.xy = u_xlat16_6.xy * vec2(u_xlat16_28);
    u_xlat16_6.xzw = u_xlat16_6.xxx * _flowFresnelColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xzw = _flowColor.xyz * _flowColor.www + u_xlat16_6.xzw;
    u_xlat16_17.x = u_xlat16_6.y * _DOTEmissionScale;
    u_xlat16_17.x = u_xlat16_17.x * _Ratio_FlashColorEffect;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat16_17.xxx * _DOTColor.xyz + u_xlat16_11.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat1.xy = u_xlat1.xx * _flowPosition.zw + u_xlat3.xy;
    u_xlat10_1.xyz = texture2D(_AdditionalTexture, u_xlat1.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat10_1.xyz * _AddTexColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_17.x = _Ratio_ExtraTexture * _AddTexScale;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * u_xlat16_17.xxx + u_xlat16_11.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xzw * vec3(vec3(_Ratio_flowColor, _Ratio_flowColor, _Ratio_flowColor)) + u_xlat16_11.xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xxx * _SteadyColor.xyz + (-u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_33 = _Ratio_SteadyColorEffect * _SteadyColor.w;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_33) * u_xlat16_0.xyz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(1.12949991, 1.12949991, 1.12949991) + vec3(0.0299999993, 0.0299999993, 0.0299999993);
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(0.449999988, 0.449999988, 0.449999988);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(1.09350002, 1.09350002, 1.09350002) + vec3(0.589999974, 0.589999974, 0.589999974);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * u_xlat2.xyz + vec3(0.0799999982, 0.0799999982, 0.0799999982);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz / u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = min(u_xlat1.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz;
    SV_Target0.w = _CustomAlpha;
    return;
}

    gl_Position = u_xlat0;

    vs_TEXCOORD6.yzw = vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0);

    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_5.x * _flowFresnelPower;

    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat0.y * u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat6 = u_xlat0.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat11 = u_xlat1.x * 0.125 + u_xlat6;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * 0.125 + (-u_xlat6);
    u_xlat1.y = u_xlat1.x + 0.125;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat11 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_2.xy = max(u_xlat1.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_2.xy = u_xlat16_2.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_1 = u_xlat16_2.yyyy * _SHBotColor;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat16_2.xxxx * _SHTopColor + u_xlat16_1;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyw = (-u_xlat4.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat0.w = u_xlat1.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat0;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat2.w = u_xlat1.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat2;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat0.zxy * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.yzx * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat4.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat4.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat4.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    u_xlat3.x = u_xlat0.z * unity_FogParams.z + unity_FogParams.w;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat3.x = min(max(u_xlat3.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat3.x = clamp(u_xlat3.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    gl_Position = u_xlat0;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.x = u_xlat3.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.yzw = vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    return;
}

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump samplerCube unity_SpecCube0;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _AdditionalTexture;
UNITY_LOCATION(2) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(3) uniform mediump sampler2D _BumpMap;
UNITY_LOCATION(4) uniform mediump sampler2D _MixMap;
UNITY_LOCATION(5) uniform mediump sampler2D _MatMap;
in highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
in highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD8;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
vec3 u_xlat0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
vec3 u_xlat1;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_1;
bool u_xlatb1;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_3;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_5;
vec3 u_xlat6;
vec3 u_xlat7;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_7;
vec3 u_xlat8;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_9;
mediump float u_xlat16_15;
mediump float u_xlat16_25;
float u_xlat31;
mediump float u_xlat16_32;
mediump float u_xlat16_33;
mediump float u_xlat16_35;
void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat1.x = _CustomAlpha * u_xlat16_0.w + (-_Cutoff0);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb1 = !!(u_xlat1.x<0.0);
#else
    u_xlatb1 = u_xlat1.x<0.0;
#endif
    if(u_xlatb1){discard;}
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_2.xy = u_xlat16_2.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_2.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyw = u_xlat16_2.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_2.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyw;
    u_xlat16_32 = dot(u_xlat16_2.xyz, u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_32 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_32);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_32) * u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_3.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_3.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = max(u_xlat1.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xxx * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_32 = dot((-u_xlat1.xyz), u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_32 + u_xlat16_32;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * (-vec3(u_xlat16_32)) + (-u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4 = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_4.y + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_32 = max(u_xlat16_32, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_32 = min(u_xlat16_32, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_33 = (-u_xlat16_32) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_33 = u_xlat16_32 * u_xlat16_33;
    u_xlat16_33 = u_xlat16_33 * 6.0;
    u_xlat16_3 = textureLod(unity_SpecCube0, u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_33);
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_3.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_5.x = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_5.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_5.x = max(u_xlat16_5.x, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_5.x = log2(u_xlat16_5.x);
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_5.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_5.x = exp2(u_xlat16_5.x);
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_5.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat16_5.xxx;
    u_xlat16_35 = u_xlat16_32 * u_xlat16_32;
    u_xlat31 = u_xlat16_35 * u_xlat16_35 + 1.0;
    u_xlat31 = float(1.0) / u_xlat31;
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * vec3(u_xlat31);
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_4.x + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_15 = (-u_xlat16_5.x) * 0.959999979 + 0.959999979;
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_5.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_5.x = min(max(u_xlat16_5.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_5.x = clamp(u_xlat16_5.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_15 = (-u_xlat16_15) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_32 = (-u_xlat16_32) + u_xlat16_15;
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_32 + 1.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_32 = min(max(u_xlat16_32, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_32 = clamp(u_xlat16_32, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xxx * u_xlat7.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = (-u_xlat16_0.xyz) * u_xlat16_5.xxx + u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    u_xlat8.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_32) + (-u_xlat7.xyz);
    u_xlat16_32 = dot(u_xlat16_2.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_32 = abs(u_xlat16_32) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_32 = min(u_xlat16_32, 1.0);
    u_xlat31 = (-u_xlat16_32) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_35 = u_xlat31 * u_xlat31;
    u_xlat16_35 = u_xlat16_35 * u_xlat16_35;
    u_xlat7.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_35) * u_xlat8.xyz + u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat6.xyz * u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat6.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz * u_xlat16_5.xyz + u_xlat6.xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = (-u_xlat1.yzx) * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].zxy;
    u_xlat7.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].yzx * (-u_xlat1.zxy) + (-u_xlat7.xyz);
    u_xlat31 = dot(u_xlat7.xyz, u_xlat7.xyz);
    u_xlat31 = inversesqrt(u_xlat31);
    u_xlat7.xyz = vec3(u_xlat31) * u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat8.xyz = (-u_xlat1.zxy) * u_xlat7.yzx;
    u_xlat8.xyz = (-u_xlat1.yzx) * u_xlat7.zxy + (-u_xlat8.xyz);
    u_xlat7.x = dot(u_xlat7.xyz, u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat7.z = dot((-u_xlat1.xyz), u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat8.xyz, u_xlat8.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xxx * u_xlat8.xyz;
    u_xlat7.y = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat16_2.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat1.x = min(max(u_xlat1.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat1.x = clamp(u_xlat1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat1.xxx * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat7.xyz, u_xlat7.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat1.xy = u_xlat1.xx * u_xlat7.xy;
    u_xlat1.xy = u_xlat1.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = texture(_MatMap, u_xlat1.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat1.xy = u_xlat1.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vs_TEXCOORD8.xy;
    u_xlat1.xy = u_xlat1.xy * _AddTexST.xy + _AddTexST.zw;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_7.xyz * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat7.xyz * vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005);
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = min(u_xlat16_9.xyz, vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005));
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat16_9.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * u_xlat16_9.xyz + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat6.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_4.w * _Emissive;
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_5.x * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * u_xlat16_5.xxx;
    u_xlat16_35 = u_xlat16_0.w * _CustomAlpha;
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat16_35;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * _EmisssionColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * u_xlat16_4.zzz + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = _TimeParameters.x * _DOTEmissionQuency;
    u_xlat0.y = _TimeParameters.x * _OverlayColorQuency;
    u_xlat0.xy = sin(u_xlat0.xy);
    u_xlat16_5.x = _OverlayColor.w + (-_OverlayColorFlicker);
    u_xlat16_15 = _OverlayColor.w + _OverlayColorFlicker;
    u_xlat16_5.x = (-u_xlat16_15) + u_xlat16_5.x;
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat0.y * u_xlat16_5.x + u_xlat16_15;
    u_xlat16_5.x = (-u_xlat16_5.x) * _Ratio_OverlayColorEffect + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * u_xlat16_5.xxx;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = _OverlayColor.xyz * vec3(_Ratio_OverlayColorEffect) + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.x = (-u_xlat16_32) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_5.x = log2(u_xlat16_5.x);
    u_xlat16_15 = u_xlat16_5.x * _DOTFresnelPower;
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_5.x * _flowFresnelPower;
    u_xlat16_5.x = exp2(u_xlat16_5.x);
    u_xlat16_5.y = exp2(u_xlat16_15);
    u_xlat16_5.xy = min(u_xlat16_5.xy, vec2(1.0, 1.0));
    u_xlat16_25 = (-_DOTEmissionMax) + _DOTEmissionMin;
    u_xlat16_25 = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat16_25 + _DOTEmissionMax;
    u_xlat16_5.xy = u_xlat16_5.xy * vec2(u_xlat16_25);
    u_xlat16_5.xzw = u_xlat16_5.xxx * _flowFresnelColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xzw = _flowColor.xyz * _flowColor.www + u_xlat16_5.xzw;
    u_xlat16_15 = u_xlat16_5.y * _DOTEmissionScale;
    u_xlat16_15 = u_xlat16_15 * _Ratio_FlashColorEffect;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_15) * _DOTColor.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xx * _flowPosition.zw + u_xlat1.xy;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = texture(_AdditionalTexture, u_xlat0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * _AddTexColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_15 = _Ratio_ExtraTexture * _AddTexScale;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_9.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_15) + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xzw * vec3(vec3(_Ratio_flowColor, _Ratio_flowColor, _Ratio_flowColor)) + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_32) * _SteadyColor.xyz + (-u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat16_32 = _Ratio_SteadyColorEffect * _SteadyColor.w;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_32) * u_xlat16_2.xyz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vec3(1.12949991, 1.12949991, 1.12949991) + vec3(0.0299999993, 0.0299999993, 0.0299999993);

    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat16_7.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz / u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = min(u_xlat0.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    return;
}

vec4 u_xlat0;

mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;

void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat0.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat0.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat0.y * u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat6 = u_xlat0.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat11 = u_xlat1.x * 0.125 + u_xlat6;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * 0.125 + (-u_xlat6);
    u_xlat1.y = u_xlat1.x + 0.125;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat11 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_2.xy = max(u_xlat1.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_2.xy = u_xlat16_2.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_1 = u_xlat16_2.yyyy * _SHBotColor;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat16_2.xxxx * _SHTopColor + u_xlat16_1;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz;

    u_xlat0.w = u_xlat1.x;

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump samplerCube unity_SpecCube0;

in highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
in highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD8;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
vec3 u_xlat0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
vec3 u_xlat1;
bool u_xlatb1;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
vec3 u_xlat3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_6;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_7;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_8;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_9;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_10;
vec3 u_xlat12;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_13;
vec3 u_xlat14;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_18;
mediump float u_xlat16_29;
float u_xlat33;
mediump float u_xlat16_35;
mediump float u_xlat16_41;
void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat1.x = _CustomAlpha * u_xlat16_0.w + (-_Cutoff0);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb1 = !!(u_xlat1.x<0.0);
#else
    u_xlatb1 = u_xlat1.x<0.0;
#endif
    if(u_xlatb1){discard;}
    u_xlat16_2.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_2.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_2.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat16_2.xyz, u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = max(u_xlat1.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat12.xyz = u_xlat1.xxx * u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * u_xlat1.xxx + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = (-u_xlat12.yzx) * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].zxy;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].yzx * (-u_xlat12.zxy) + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat1.xxx * u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = (-u_xlat12.zxy) * u_xlat4.yzx;
    u_xlat5.xyz = (-u_xlat12.yzx) * u_xlat4.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat1.xxx * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_2.xy = u_xlat16_2.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_2.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyw = u_xlat16_2.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_7.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_2.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyw;
    u_xlat16_35 = dot(u_xlat16_2.xyz, u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_35 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_35);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_35) * u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat5.y = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat5.x = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat5.z = dot((-u_xlat12.xyz), u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat4.xy = u_xlat1.xx * u_xlat5.xy;
    u_xlat4.xy = u_xlat4.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = texture(_MatMap, u_xlat4.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat4.xy = u_xlat4.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vs_TEXCOORD8.xy;
    u_xlat4.xy = u_xlat4.xy * _AddTexST.xy + _AddTexST.zw;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat1.xxx * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat16_2.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat1.x = min(max(u_xlat1.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat1.x = clamp(u_xlat1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat3.x = (-u_xlat1.x) * u_xlat1.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_6 = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_35 = u_xlat16_6.y + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_35 = max(u_xlat16_35, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_35 = min(u_xlat16_35, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_7.x = u_xlat16_35 * u_xlat16_35;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * u_xlat16_7.x;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * u_xlat1.x + u_xlat3.x;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat16_7.x / u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat3.x = u_xlat16_7.x * u_xlat16_7.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat3.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat3.x;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat14.x = u_xlat16_35 * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * u_xlat14.x;
    u_xlat1.x = min(u_xlat1.x, 100.0);
    u_xlat14.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_7.x = u_xlat16_6.x + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_18.x = u_xlat16_7.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_18.x = min(max(u_xlat16_18.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_18.x = clamp(u_xlat16_18.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_7.x = (-u_xlat16_7.x) * 0.959999979 + 0.959999979;
    u_xlat16_7.x = (-u_xlat16_7.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_7.x = (-u_xlat16_35) + u_xlat16_7.x;
    u_xlat16_7.x = u_xlat16_7.x + 1.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_7.x = min(max(u_xlat16_7.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else

SubProgram "gles " {
"// hash: 646e16e91365991e
#ifdef VERTEX
#version 100

uniform 	vec3 _WorldSpaceCameraPos;
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[4];
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[4];
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[4];
uniform 	float _Offset1;
uniform 	float _Offset2;
uniform 	float _UBuffWidth;
attribute highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
attribute highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
attribute highp vec4 in_COLOR0;
varying highp float vs_TEXCOORD0;
vec3 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
float u_xlat6;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.x = ceil(in_COLOR0.w);
    u_xlat0.x = (-u_xlat0.x) + in_COLOR0.w;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat0.x = (-u_xlat0.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * 0.0500000007;
    u_xlat2.x = _Offset1 + _Offset2;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat2.x * 0.00999999978 + (-u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat2.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, in_NORMAL0.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat2.xxx * in_NORMAL0.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz * vec3(vec3(_UBuffWidth, _UBuffWidth, _UBuffWidth)) + in_POSITION0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat2.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * u_xlat2.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * u_xlat2.zzz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat2.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat2.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat2.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat2.xyz = (-u_xlat2.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x / u_xlat1.w;
    gl_Position.z = (-u_xlat0.x) + u_xlat1.z;
    gl_Position.xyw = u_xlat1.xyw;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);

#if UNITY_SUPPORTS_UNIFORM_LOCATION

#endif
uniform 	vec3 _WorldSpaceCameraPos;
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[4];
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
UNITY_BINDING(1) uniform UnityPerDraw {
#endif
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[4];
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[4];
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 unity_LODFade;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_WorldTransformParams;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_LightData;

#endif
	UNITY_UNIFORM float _LineColorPosi;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec3 _LineConstColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM float _TexorColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _CustomAlpha;
	UNITY_UNIFORM float _Offset1;
	UNITY_UNIFORM float _Offset2;
	UNITY_UNIFORM float _UBuffWidth;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 _OutlineColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 _lightDir;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Rim;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
};
#endif
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_COLOR0;
out highp float vs_TEXCOORD0;
vec3 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
float u_xlat6;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.x = ceil(in_COLOR0.w);
    u_xlat0.x = (-u_xlat0.x) + in_COLOR0.w;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x + 1.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat0.x = min(max(u_xlat0.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat0.x = (-u_xlat0.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * 0.0500000007;
    u_xlat2.x = _Offset1 + _Offset2;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat2.x * 0.00999999978 + (-u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat2.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, in_NORMAL0.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat2.xxx * in_NORMAL0.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz * vec3(vec3(_UBuffWidth, _UBuffWidth, _UBuffWidth)) + in_POSITION0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat2.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * u_xlat2.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * u_xlat2.zzz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat2.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat2.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat2.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat2.xyz = (-u_xlat2.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x / u_xlat1.w;
    gl_Position.z = (-u_xlat0.x) + u_xlat1.z;
    gl_Position.xyw = u_xlat1.xyw;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat6 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat6 = max(u_xlat6, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat6 = inversesqrt(u_xlat6);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat6) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD0 = dot((-u_xlat1.xyz), u_xlat0.xyz);
    return;
}

#endif

    u_xlat0.x = _Time.y * _LineColorSpeed + _LineColorPosi;
    u_xlat0.x = fract(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.y = 0.5;

    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz + (-_LineConstColor.xyz);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(_TexorColor) * u_xlat0.xyz + _LineConstColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.w = vs_TEXCOORD0 * vs_TEXCOORD0;
    SV_Target0 = u_xlat0;

#define HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS 1
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
#define UNITY_UNIFORM
#else
#define UNITY_UNIFORM uniform
#endif
#define UNITY_SUPPORTS_UNIFORM_LOCATION 1
#if UNITY_SUPPORTS_UNIFORM_LOCATION
#define UNITY_LOCATION(x) layout(location = x)
#define UNITY_BINDING(x) layout(binding = x, std140)
#else
#define UNITY_LOCATION(x)
#define UNITY_BINDING(x) layout(std140)
#endif
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[4];
uniform 	vec4 _ShadowBias;
uniform 	vec3 _LightDirection;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
UNITY_BINDING(1) uniform UnityPerDraw {
#endif
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[4];
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[4];
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 unity_LODFade;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_WorldTransformParams;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_LightData;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_LightIndices[2];
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 unity_ProbesOcclusion;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SpecCube0_HDR;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 unity_LightmapST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 unity_DynamicLightmapST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHAr;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHAg;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHAb;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHBr;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHBg;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHBb;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHC;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
};
#endif
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
UNITY_BINDING(0) uniform UnityPerMaterial {
#endif
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _MainTex_ST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _BumpMap_ST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _BaseColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Emissive;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _RoughNessOffset;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _SpecularColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _MetallicOffset;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _NormalScale;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _EmisssionScale;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _SHScale;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _SHTopColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _SHBotColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Metallic;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Smoothness;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Cutoff;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec3 _AddLightDir;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _AddlightColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _CustomAlpha;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Ratio_SteadyColorEffect;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _SteadyColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Ratio_FlashColorEffect;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _DOTEmissionQuency;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _DOTColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _DOTFresnelPower;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _DOTEmissionMax;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _DOTEmissionMin;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _OverlayColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _OverlayColorQuency;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _OverlayColorFlicker;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Ratio_OverlayColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _DOTEmissionScale;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Ratio_OverlayColorEffect;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _MouthTiling;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _MouthOffset;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _EyeTiling;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _EyeOffset;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 _AddTexST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _AddTexColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _AddTexScale;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Ratio_ExtraTexture;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _flowColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _flowPosition;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _flowFresnelPower;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _flowFresnelColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _flowFilp;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Ratio_flowColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _PostUVFlip;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 _FaceOffset;
	UNITY_UNIFORM float _ChangeFace;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _EmisssionColor;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
};
#endif
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
float u_xlat6;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = _LightDirection.xyz * _ShadowBias.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat6 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat6 = max(u_xlat6, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat6 = inversesqrt(u_xlat6);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat6) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat6 = dot(_LightDirection.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat6 = min(max(u_xlat6, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat6 = clamp(u_xlat6, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat6 = (-u_xlat6) + 1.0;
    u_xlat6 = u_xlat6 * _ShadowBias.y;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * vec3(u_xlat6) + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    gl_Position.z = max((-u_xlat0.w), u_xlat0.z);
    gl_Position.xyw = u_xlat0.xyw;
    return;
}

#endif

#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
};
#endif
UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainTex;
in highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_TARGET0;
mediump float u_xlat16_0;
bool u_xlatb0;
mediump float u_xlat16_1;
void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).w;
    u_xlat16_1 = u_xlat16_0 + (-_Cutoff);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb0 = !!(u_xlat16_1<0.0);
#else
    u_xlatb0 = u_xlat16_1<0.0;
#endif
    if(u_xlatb0){discard;}
    SV_TARGET0 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    return;
}
